Department of 
Wind Energy 
Master Report 
 
 
 
Structural topology optimization of wind turbine 
blades 
 
 
Georgios Siskos 
DTU Wind Energy-M-0079 
June 2016 
==PAGE:2==
 Authors: Georgios Siskos 
Title: Structural topology optimization of wind turbine blades 
Summary:  
The project delves into 3D topology optimization of beam-like 
structures. A beam finite element model is implemented while 
parallel computing is employed to reduce the computation cost. 
The optimal design problem consists of two main formulations: 
the maximization of the minimum natural frequency and the 
maximization of gap between constitutive natural frequency 
subsets, subject to global volume constraints. An aggregation 
function is used to formulate the objective function while an 
interior point algorithm is employed in optimization procedure.  
The optimal design is applied in a typical rectangular beam 
considering different kind of material properties and boundary 
conditions while multi-material scheme is also implemented. The 
derived topology layouts are presented in 2D figures and 3D 
visualization plots along with the corresponding mode shapes and 
natural frequency magnitudes. In order to enhance the continuity 
between constitutive cross sections a 3D filter is developed. 
According to the numerical experiments the overall response has 
met the expectations. However, further development is required in 
order to cope with the size and requirements of the 3D 
optimization design of wind turbine blades with respect to the 
current optimization problem formulation. 
 
DTU Wind Energy-M-0079 
June 2016 
Project Period: January – June 2016 
 
 
ECTS: 30

==PAGE:101==
 
 
DTU Wind Energy is a department of the Technical University of Denmark with a unique integration of research, education, innovation and 
public/private sector consulting in the field of wind energy. Our activities develop new opportunities and technology for the global and Danish 
exploitation of wind energy. Research focuses on key technical-scientific fields, which are central for the development, innovation and use of wind 
energy and provides the basis for advanced education at the education. 
 
We have more than 240 staff members of which approximately 60 are PhD students. Research is conducted within nine research programmes 
organized into three main topics: Wind energy systems, Wind turbine technology and Basics for wind energy. 
 
Technical University of Denmark 
Department of Wind Energy 
Frederiksborgvej 399 
4000 Roskilde 
Denmark
